</style><script type="application/ld+json" data-next-head="">{"@context":"https://schema.org","@type":"BlogPosting","datePublished":"11/11/2020, 8:39:37 PM","description":"&amp;nbsp;\nLeveraging Indictors of Compromise (IOC) and searching historical data for attack patterns is one of the primary responsibilities of a security monitoring&amp;nbsp;team. Relevant&amp;nbsp;security&amp;nbsp;data for threat hunting/investigation related to&amp;nbsp;an&amp;nbsp;enterprise&amp;nbsp;is produced in multiple locations -&amp;nbsp;cloud,&amp;nbsp;on-premises, and being able to analyze all the data from a single point makes it easier to spot trends and attack. Azure Sentinel has made it super easy to collect data from multiple logs&amp;nbsp;across different environments&amp;nbsp;and run&amp;nbsp;KQL&amp;nbsp;queries of recently released threat indicators&amp;nbsp;across&amp;nbsp;this&amp;nbsp;entire data set.&amp;nbsp;For example, through its recently released&amp;nbsp;Microsoft 365 Defender&amp;nbsp;connector&amp;nbsp;security teams can now easily ingest&amp;nbsp;Microsoft 365 data into Azure Sentinel&amp;nbsp;allowing&amp;nbsp;correlation of M365 raw logs with Sentinel’s additional data sources to provide additional insights for investigations, hunting and alerts.&amp;nbsp;In this blog post we share some of the IOC’s&amp;nbsp;related to&amp;nbsp;one such threat actor that Microsoft tracks as Barium&amp;nbsp;and the sample Azure Sentinel queries&amp;nbsp;related to it&amp;nbsp;that leverage multiple logs including those coming from Microsoft 365 Defender connector&amp;nbsp;.\n&amp;nbsp;\nAbout a month and a half ago,&amp;nbsp;the&amp;nbsp;US&amp;nbsp;Department of Justice, Office of Public Affairs, released&amp;nbsp;documents&amp;nbsp;detailing work&amp;nbsp;done&amp;nbsp;by a range of public and&amp;nbsp;private sector&amp;nbsp;organizations,&amp;nbsp;including&amp;nbsp;Microsoft,&amp;nbsp;to disrupt&amp;nbsp;Barium’s&amp;nbsp;cyberattack&amp;nbsp;infrastructure.&amp;nbsp;Barium is&amp;nbsp;intent&amp;nbsp;on compromising&amp;nbsp;research and development (R&amp;amp;D) heavy organizations in telecom, high tech,&amp;nbsp;computer,&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;healthcare;&amp;nbsp;their&amp;nbsp;financially motivated operations&amp;nbsp;have&amp;nbsp;focused primarily on the video game industry.&amp;nbsp;The techniques that the group have used in the past&amp;nbsp;have&amp;nbsp;varied from using malicious .lnk&amp;nbsp;files,&amp;nbsp;Word&amp;nbsp;and PowerPoint macros, to the use of&amp;nbsp;open-source&amp;nbsp;tools like Cobalt strike to achieve their&amp;nbsp;objective. The group has been pretty prolific in the use of “supply chain” attacks to compromise software providers and then modify the providers’ code to facilitate further intrusions against its customers. They have also been seen using&amp;nbsp;C2&amp;nbsp;“dead drops,” which are&amp;nbsp;seemingly legitimate&amp;nbsp;web pages that have encoded instructions to their malware. &amp;nbsp;In their campaign they have also been seen using typo-squatted domains to impersonate legitimate companies and products.&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;\n&amp;nbsp;\nMicrosoft Threat Intelligence Center (MSTIC) along with partner teams have been tracking and gathering information on Barium,&amp;nbsp;monitoring&amp;nbsp;the group’s&amp;nbsp;activities&amp;nbsp;as they&amp;nbsp;operate&amp;nbsp;a&amp;nbsp;number&amp;nbsp;of&amp;nbsp;websites,&amp;nbsp;domains&amp;nbsp;and internet-connected computers.&amp;nbsp;You can read more about this in&amp;nbsp;the September&amp;nbsp;2020&amp;nbsp;Microsoft Digital Defense report.\n&amp;nbsp;\nMSTIC&amp;nbsp;has now shared&amp;nbsp;many&amp;nbsp;of these indicators (IP/domains) so that you can&amp;nbsp;hunt&amp;nbsp;for them&amp;nbsp;in Azure Sentinel&amp;nbsp;using relevant data&amp;nbsp;like&amp;nbsp;the newly integrated&amp;nbsp;Microsoft 365&amp;nbsp;Defender&amp;nbsp;data,&amp;nbsp;DNS logs,&amp;nbsp;Firewall data etc.&amp;nbsp;Microsoft 365 E5 customers, now also have the advantage of getting Azure credits towards Microsoft 365 data ingestion into Azure Sentinel - see https://aka.ms/m365-sentinel-offer&amp;nbsp; for details. With this new offer, you can take advantage of end-to-end integrated security and save significant costs when ingesting Microsoft 365 data into Azure Sentinel.&amp;nbsp;\n&amp;nbsp;\nBelow are sample data-contrast="none"><SPAN class="NormalTextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8"><SPAN>&nbsp;</SPAN>files,<SPAN>&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="TextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-contrast="none"><SPAN PowerPoint macros, to the use of<SPAN>&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="TextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-contrast="none"><SPAN class="NormalTextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8">open-source</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="TextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-contrast="none"><SPAN class="NormalTextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8"><SPAN>&nbsp;</SPAN>tools like Cobalt strike to achieve their<SPAN>&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="TextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-contrast="none"><SPAN class="NormalTextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8">objective</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="TextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-contrast="none"><SPAN class="NormalTextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8">. The group has been pretty prolific in the use of “supply chain” attacks to compromise software providers and then modify the providers’ code to facilitate further intrusions against its customers. They have also been seen using<SPAN>&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="TextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-contrast="none"><SPAN class="NormalTextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8">C2</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="TextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-contrast="none"><SPAN class="NormalTextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8"><SPAN>&nbsp;</SPAN>“dead drops,” which are<SPAN>&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="TextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-contrast="none"><SPAN class="NormalTextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8">seemingly legitimate</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="TextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-contrast="none"><SPAN class="NormalTextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8"><SPAN>&nbsp;</SPAN>web pages that have encoded instructions to their malware</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="TextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-contrast="none"><SPAN class="NormalTextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8">. &nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="TextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-contrast="none"><SPAN class="NormalTextRun SCXW253407441 BCX8">In their campaign they have also been seen using typo-squatted domains to impersonate legitimate companies and products.<SPAN>&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN class="EOP TrackedChange SCXW253407441 BCX8" data-ccp-props="{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559739&quot;:160,&quot;335559740&quot;:259}">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P>&nbsp;</P>
